GT Equivalence Verification (CRK32)
============================================================
GT: -c0*A - c1*A*exp(-c2*_s*t) + c3*_f*A**c4
Candidate formulas: 51

GT is the fixed function
\[
0.7991114344496316\,A^{1/3}\;-\;0.49947326957917104\,A\;-\;0.49947326957917104\,A\,e^{-0.050569865727257013\,t}.
\]
So any matching candidate must be able to represent **exactly**: (i) an \(A^{1/3}\) term with constant coefficient, (ii) a linear \(-A\) term, (iii) a linear-in-\(A\) exponential-in-\(t\) term with coefficient \(-A\cdot 0.49947...\) and exponent \(-0.05056...t\), and **no other nonzero dependence** on \(t\) or \(A\).

---

### 1.
Has \(A c0 e^{c1 t}\) (good shape), plus \(A c2\sin(\cdot)\), plus \(A^{c5}c6\), plus constants and extra \(e^{c9 t}\). You can zero out the sine and extra exp and constant terms, and set \(c5=1/3\). But then you still need a separate \(-0.49947A\) term: not present unless you use \(A^{c5}c6\) with \(c5=1\), which would break the \(A^{1/3}\) requirement. So cannot get both \(A^{1/3}\) and \(A\) simultaneously. **No match**.

### 2.
Contains \(c4( |A|+1)^{c5}\) and \(c7(|A|+1)^{c8}\) which must be zeroed to avoid non-polynomial-in-\(A\) behavior. Then it becomes \(c0A^{1/3}+A c1 e^{c2 t}+A c3 + c6\). Set \(c6=0\), choose \(c0=0.799111...\), \(c3=-0.499473...\), \(c1=-0.499473...\), \(c2=-0.0505698...\). This exactly matches GT. **Match**.

### 3.
Has extra \(A c4 e^{A c5}\) which must be removed by setting \(c4=0\). Then same core as (2) with an extra constant \(c6\) set to 0. Can match GT by same parameter choices. **Match**.

### 4.
Has extra \(c4 e^{c5 t}\) (not multiplied by \(A\)); must set \(c4=0\). Then same core as (2) plus constant \(c6\to 0\). Can match GT. **Match**.

### 5.
Has extra \(c4\) and \(c5 t (A+c6)^{c7}\). Must set \(c4=0\) and \(c5=0\) to remove them. Then same core as (2) with no extra constant term. Can match GT. **Match**.

### 6.
Form: \(A c0 e^{c1 t} + A c2 + A^{c3}c4 + c5 + c6 e^{c7 t}\).
To get \(A^{1/3}\) set \(c3=1/3\), \(c4=0.799111...\). To get \(-0.49947A\) set \(c2=-0.499473...\). To get \(-0.49947A e^{-kt}\) set \(c0=-0.499473...\), \(c1=-0.0505698...\). Must also remove \(c5\) and \(c6 e^{c7 t}\) by setting \(c5=0,c6=0\). Works. **Match**.

### 7.
Has extra rational terms in \(A\): \(c4 t/(A c5+c6)+c7/(A c5+c6)+c8\). Must eliminate by setting \(c4=0,c7=0,c8=0\). Then core matches (2). **Match**.

### 8.
Has extra \(c4 t^{c5}\) which must be zeroed via \(c4=0\), and constant \(c6=0\). Then core matches. **Match**.

### 9.
Has extra \(A c4 (c5+t)^{c6}\). Only way to remove for all \(t\) is \(c4=0\). Then core matches, with \(c7=0\). **Match**.

### 10.
Has extra \(c4 e^{A c5}\) (not in GT). Must set \(c4=0\), \(c6=0\). Then core matches. **Match**.

### 11.
Has extra \(c4 + c5 t\). Must set \(c4=0,c5=0\). Then core matches. **Match**.

### 12.
Has extra \(\frac{A c4}{A c5+c6}+\frac{c7}{A c5+c6}+c8\). Must set \(c4=0,c7=0,c8=0\). Then core matches. **Match**.

### 13.
Has extra \(\frac{c4 t}{c5 t+c6}+\frac{c7}{c5 t+c6}+c8\). Must set \(c4=0,c7=0,c8=0\). Then core matches. **Match**.

### 14.
Has extra \(c4\log(c5 t+1)+c6\). Must set \(c4=0,c6=0\). Then core matches. **Match**.

### 15.
Form: \(c0A^{1/3}+A c1 + A c2 e^{c3 t}+ c4\tanh(c5 t+c6)+c7\).
Need to remove tanh and constant: set \(c4=0,c7=0\). Then choose \(c1=-0.499473...\), \(c2=-0.499473...\), \(c3=-0.0505698...\), \(c0=0.799111...\). Works. **Match**.

### 16.
Has \(A c3 + A c4\) redundant linear terms plus constant \(c5\). Set \(c5=0\) and choose \(c3+c4=-0.499473...\). Exponential term and \(A^{1/3}\) term can be set as needed. Works. **Match**.

### 17.
Has \(c3\) constant and \(c4|A c5|\) absolute value term. Must set \(c3=0\) and \(c4=0\) (or \(c5=0\)) to remove. Then it lacks the plain \(-0.49947A\) term (only has \(A c1 e^{c2 t}\) plus \(A^{1/3}\)). No way to create an additional linear-in-\(A\) non-exponential term. **No match**.

### 18.
\(c0A^{1/3}+A c1 e^{c2 t}+A c3 + c4\). Set \(c4=0\) and choose coefficients/exponent to match GT. **Match**.

### 19.
\(A c0 e^{c1 t}+A c2 + c3 + c4\max(0,A)^{1/3}\).
Even if \(c3=0\), \(\max(0,A)^{1/3}\) is not equal to \(A^{1/3}\) for negative \(A\). Since equivalence must hold for all real \(A\), cannot match GT’s \(A^{1/3}\). **No match**.

### 20.
Has extra \(A c4(\,c5|A|+c6|A|^2+1\,)^{c7}+c8\). Must set \(c4=0,c8=0\). Then core matches. **Match**.

### 21.
Exactly the core \(c0A^{1/3}+A c1 e^{c2 t}+A c3\). Choose \(c0=0.799111...\), \(c3=-0.499473...\), \(c1=-0.499473...\), \(c2=-0.0505698...\). **Match**.

### 22.
Has extra \(c4\sin(A c5+c6)+c7\). Must set \(c4=0,c7=0\). Then core matches. **Match**.

### 23.
Has extra \(A^{c4}c5+c6\). To avoid extra constant set \(c6=0\). But then you’d have two power terms: \(A^{1/3}\) and \(A^{c4}\). To match GT, either set \(c5=0\) (remove it) or set \(c4=1/3\) and absorb into \(c0\). Either way you can still match the needed linear \(A\) and \(A e^{c2 t}\) terms. **Match**.

### 24.
\(A c0 e^{c1 t}+A c2 e^{c3 t}+A^{c4}c5+c6+c7 e^{c8 t}\).
Need exactly one \(A e^{(\cdot)t}\) term and no pure \(e^{(\cdot)t}\). Set \(c7=0,c6=0\). Set one of the \(A e^{...}\) terms to be the GT exponential and kill the other by setting its coefficient to 0 (e.g., \(c2=0\)). Set \(c4=1/3,c5=0.799111...\) and add linear \(-0.49947A\) is missing unless you use the remaining \(A e^{...}\) with exponent 0 (i.e., \(c3=0\)) and coefficient \(-0.49947\), while the other \(A e^{...}\) uses exponent \(-0.05056\). That works. **Match**.

### 25.
Has extra \(c4\log(A c5+1)+c6\). Must set \(c4=0,c6=0\). Then core matches. **Match**.

### 26.
\(A c0 + A c1 e^{c2 t} + A^{c3}c4 + c5\log(A c6+1)+c7\).
Must set \(c5=0,c7=0\). Then choose \(c3=1/3,c4=0.799111...\), \(c0=-0.499473...\), \(c1=-0.499473...\), \(c2=-0.0505698...\). **Match**.

### 27.
Has extra \(A c4|A|+c5\). Must set \(c4=0,c5=0\). Then core matches. **Match**.

### 28.
Has extra \(A c4(|A|c5+1)^{c6}+c7\). Must set \(c4=0,c7=0\). Then core matches. **Match**.

### 29.
\(A c0 e^{c1 t}+A^{c2}c3+c4+c5 e^{c6 t}+c7|A c8|\).
Absolute value term must be removed: set \(c7=0\). Pure exponential must be removed: set \(c5=0\). Constant \(c4=0\). Then you have \(A c0 e^{c1 t}+A^{c2}c3\): cannot produce both \(A^{1/3}\) and linear \(A\) and also the \(A e^{-kt}\) term simultaneously (only one \(A e^{...}\) term and one power term). If power term used for \(A^{1/3}\), no linear \(A\). If used for linear \(A\), no \(A^{1/3}\). **No match**.

### 30.
Includes \(A^2 c0\) which must be zeroed: set \(c0=0\). Also has extra \(A^{c4}c5\) and \(c7 e^{c8 t}\) and constant \(c6\).
